name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr

posted:Posted February 21, 2024
msg:Advantages: The room is large and very close to the beach. Walk out of the hotel and cross the non-motorized road to the beach. There are camping tents for rent on the beach. You can sing there at night. The hotel configuration is very high. Many places in the room are designed with arcs to avoid injury due to bumps. This is done very well. Every room in the entire hotel has a balcony and bathtub. There is a door between the washing area and the room, but it is invisible. We didn't discover it until we stayed for two days. The hotel has beach slippers for adults and children. The quality is good. I didn't even wear the ones I brought. Children's bathrobes and toiletries are available. You need to call the front desk to ask for it. We came in late February, and although the outdoor swimming pools were not open, there were three indoor swimming pools. A regular large professional swimming pool with a cooler water temperature. There are two shallow pools for children to play in. The water temperature is on the higher side. The staff requires you to wear a shower cap and swimsuit before swimming in the water. The children had so much fun that they couldn't bear to leave. There are rest chairs, stools and lounge chairs nearby. The women's locker room is very well equipped, with a dedicated locker room and a sauna room, which is so unexpected. Dry bucket of mineral water on bath towel. All these basic configurations are available. The gym is also very good and has a boxing room. The children's indoor children's playground is large, but there are relatively few games. There is an ocean ball pool and a simple small slide. There is also a children's playground outside, with slides and the like. Because my two kids came here for the beach and swimming pool. I didn‚Äôt play in the children‚Äôs playground, so I didn‚Äôt take any pictures.
Breakfast is average, breakfast time is 7:00-11:00, and can be packed into the room. Just outside the hotel gate, there are many restaurants and small shops on the next slope. There is also a cinema. Walk a few more steps and you'll see a sunny town. Milk tea, coffee, KFC, McDonald's, Western food and Chinese food are all available at Weiyou on the fourth floor. The price is moderate, the taste is good, and the portion is very large. When ordering, be sure to order less. If there is not enough, add more. There are many roadside stalls at night.
Service: The service attitude is very good. The front desk, room attendants, and restaurant waiters are all very good. Meets the service standards of a five-star hotel. Special thanks to front desk manager Quin and acting duty manager Manager Hao. There are several other staff members and a young lady pushing a wheelchair. Special thanks to. They all took special care of me after I got injured. Let me feel some warmth in the pain. Thank you so much.
Disadvantages: The only disadvantage is also the fatal flaw. The balcony design is unreasonable. It almost broke me. At 12 o'clock in the evening, I was accompanied by hotel staff to the hospital to take a film. The doctor diagnosed a fracture of the tail vertebrae. Let me talk about the problem. First, the lighting on the balcony at night is very, very dim, almost non-existent. It's a modern design. There was water underground at night, and the floor tiles were black and couldn't be seen at all. Second, the clothes drying rack is opposite to the floor drain, and the floor drain is located in the corner near the door of the room. Watch the video. The water dripping from washing clothes flows down the slope to the floor and will pass through the entire balcony, especially the balcony and the doorway of the room. Third, the cotton mops provided by the hotel are not anti-slip. Fourth, there are no instructions to be careful about slipping on the balcony. Let‚Äôs talk about what happened. The balcony was very dark at night, and the water dripping from drying clothes flowed down the slope to the floor drain. Due to unreasonable design problems, a large area of ‚Äã‚Äã‚Äã‚Äãthe balcony was covered with water. The fireworks outside were beautiful. I was wearing the cotton mop provided by the hotel. When I walked to the center of the balcony, where there was a lot of water, I suddenly slipped and fell. When I got up, I felt something was wrong. I immediately took photos and videos of the scene and called the hotel. Someone will take care of it soon. After the incident happened, the hotel's service attitude was very good, but its attitude towards compensation was average at first. Later, it improved after calling the police and communicating with the hotel. Due to a fractured tail vertebrae and unable to move, the hotel compensated for free extension of stay and meals. Medical expenses, rehabilitation expenses, lost work time, etc. are all paid by the insurance company. This kind of star-rated hotels all buy insurance for their guests.
Suggestion: After my incident, I hope the hotel can rectify the safety hazards on all balconies. I don't want anyone else to be hurt like me. When traveling, not only do you get injured but you can‚Äôt go anywhere. I'm also afraid of the side effects. I hope this safety hazard has been resolved when I come to stay next time.
Just because of the service attitude and configuration, I will try the outdoor swimming pool next time. Get a feel for Little Sanya.

Let me talk about the advantages first:
1. The price/performance ratio is very high, the room is very large, and the facilities are new, nice and beautiful
2. The surrounding environment is good, and it belongs to the high-end area. According to the locals, it belongs to the outside of the island. There are indoor and outdoor swimming pools. There is a beach outside the hotel, and the sand is very fine, which cannot be seen on the island.
3. The breakfast is rich and the noodles are delicious. There is a sunny town outside the hotel, a lot of food, and a lively night market at night.
Not enough to say:

For breakfast, no one took the initiative to ask if they want coffee or tea. The funniest thing is that there may be a lot of people during the summer vacation, there is no place for breakfast for a while, and there was only one staff member at one time. Not to mention that no one came to ask what you need, and no one even cleared the table.
2. Because it is outside the island, it is a bit troublesome to go to the central attractions. It takes a lot of time to take a taxi and the fare is not cheap. One night I took a taxi from Zengcuo'an and it cost nearly 90, which was the most economical car. Therefore, it is recommended to spend two nights on the island, and then stay here after playing almost.
3. It is still a service, which is also a small episode. I booked for three consecutive nights at the beginning, and later canceled the one-night trip to Gulangyu and changed it to Renaissance. When we checked in, we clearly said that it was ready, but when we came back from Gulangyu for a day, we finally walked to the room (our room was the farthest from the elevator) and found that the card could not be used. Immediately went to the front desk again, and ran back to the room after finishing it, only to find that they hadn't cleaned it up again. Thinking about playing outside for a day, it was hot and uncomfortable, and I wanted to take a shower and rest right away, but I didn't clean up anything. So I said that although this is a five-star hotel, the location and facilities are excellent, but the service has a long way to go.
